## String References

- **7231**: Go where?(+List scrolls down) [Stay here./San d'Oria./Windurst./Ghelsba lift./Valley of hot springs./Ronfaure Forest.]
- **7236**: Compared to San d'Oria, with its legendary orders of knights, or Windurst, with its ancient institutes of magic, Bastok is still but a newborn nation.
- **7237**: But advanced technology and near limitless underground resources have allowed Bastok to rival the other two nations in power.
- **7238**: Innovative and adaptable Humes make up more than half the population of Bastok.
- **7239**: With their flair for industry, economy, and politics, they were the driving force behind Bastok's rapid growth. Even now, Humes hold key positions in those areas.
- **7240**: The Galka, a race of hulking humanoids, comprise a third of Bastok's population. Originally hailing from Zepwell, they came to this land over six hundred years ago.
- **7241**: Without their incomparable strength, the countless ore mines that drive Bastok's economy would never have been dug.
- **7242**: Adventurers seeking fame and fortune flock to rising nations like Bastok. You are one of them.
- **7243**: Your story begins here, amid the smoke and bustle of the industrial city of Bastok.
